*schedule {\n   143→\tconst minMaxAttempts = int64(1)\n   144→\tif cfg.RetryConfig.MaxAttempts < minMaxAttempts {\n   145→\t\tcfg.Log.Warn(\"Invalid scheduler maxAttempts, using a safe minimum\", \"configured\", cfg.RetryConfig.MaxAttempts, \"actual\", minMaxAttempts)\n   146→\t\tcfg.RetryConfig.MaxAttempts = minMaxAttempts\n   147→\t}\n   148→\n   149→\tsch := schedule{\n   150→\t\tregistry:               newRuleRegistry(),\n   151→\t\tretryConfig:            cfg.RetryConfig,\n   152→\t\tclock:                  cfg.C,\n   153→\t\tbaseInterval:           cfg.BaseInterval,\n   154→\t\tlog: 174→\n   175→func (sch *schedule) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n   176→\tsch.log.Info(\"Starting scheduler\", \"tickInterval\", sch.baseInterval, \"maxAttempts\", sch.retryConfig.MaxAttempts)\n   177→\tt := ticker.New(sch.clock, sch.baseInterval, sch.metrics.Ticker, sch.log)\n   178→\tdefer t.Stop()\n   179→\n   180→\tif err := sch.schedulePeriodic(ctx, t); err != nil {\n   181→\t\tsch.log.Error(\"Failure while running the rule evaluation loop\", \"error\", err)\n   182→\t}\n   183→\treturn nil\n   184→}\n   185→\n   186→// Rules fetches the entire set of rules considered for evaluation by the scheduler on the next tick.\n   187→// Such rules are not guaranteed to have been evaluated by the scheduler.\n   188→// Rules returns all supplementary metadata for the rules that is stored by the scheduler - namely, the set of folder titles.\n   189→func (sch *schedule) Rules() ([]*ngmodels.AlertRule, map[ngmodels.FolderKey]string) {\n   190→\treturn sch.schedulableAlertRules.all()\n   191→}\n   192→\n   193→// Status fetches the health of a given scheduled rule, by key.\n   194→func (sch *schedule) Status(key ngmodels.AlertRuleKey) (ngmodels.RuleStatus, bool) {\n   195→\tif rule, ok := sch.registry.get(key); ok {\n   196→\t\treturn rule.Status(), true\n   197→\t}\n   198→\treturn ngmodels.RuleStatus{}, false\n   199→}\n   200→\n   201→// deleteAlertRule stops evaluation of the rule, deletes it from active rules, and cleans up state cache.\n   202→func (sch *schedule) deleteAlertRule(ctx context.Context, keys ...ngmodels.AlertRuleKey) {\n   203→\tfor _, key := range keys {\n   204→\t\t// It can happen that the scheduler has deleted the alert rule before the\n   205→\t\t// Ruler API has called DeleteAlertRule. This can happen as requests to\n   206→\t\t// the Ruler API do not hold an exclusive lock over all scheduler operations.\n   207→\t\t_, ok := sch.schedulableAlertRules.del(key)\n   208→\t\tif !ok {\n   209→\t\t\tsch.log.Info(\"Alert rule cannot be removed from the scheduler as it is not scheduled\", key.LogContext()...)\n   210→\t\t}\n   211→\t\t// Delete the rule routine\n   212→\t\truleRoutine, ok := sch.registry.del(key)\n   213→\t\tif !ok {\n   214→\t\t\tsch.log.Info(\"Alert rule cannot be stopped as it is not running\", key.LogContext()...)\n   215→\t\t\tcontinue\n   216→\t\t}\n   217→\n   218→\t\t// stop rule evaluation\n   219→\t\treason := sch.getRuleStopReason(ctx, ruleRoutine.Identifier())\n   220→\t\truleRoutine.Stop(reason)\n   221→\t}\n   222→\t// Our best bet at this point is that we update the metrics with what we hope to schedule in the next tick.\n   223→\talertRules, _ := sch.schedulableAlertRules.all()\n   224→\tsch.updateRulesMetrics(alertRules)\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→func (sch *schedule) getRuleStopReason(ctx context.Context, key ngmodels.AlertRuleKeyWithGroup) error {\n   228→\t// If the ruleStopReasonProvider is defined, we will use it to get the reason why the\n   229→\t// alert rule was stopped. If it returns an error, we will use the default reason.\n   230→\tif sch.ruleStopReasonProvider == nil {\n   231→\t\treturn errRuleDeleted\n   232→\t}\n   233→\n   234→\tstopReason, err := sch.ruleStopReasonProvider.FindReason(ctx, sch.log, key)\n   235→\tif err != nil {\n   236→\t\tsch.log.New(key.LogContext()...).Error(\"Failed to get stop reason\", \"error\", err)\n   237→\t\treturn errRuleDeleted\n   238→\t}\n   239→\tif stopReason == nil {\n   240→\t\treturn errRuleDeleted\n   241→\t}\n   242→\n   243→\treturn stopReason\n   244→}\n   245→\n   246→func (sch *schedule) schedulePeriodic(ctx context.Context, t *ticker.T) error {\n   247→\tdispatcherGroup, ctx := errgroup.WithContext(ctx)\n   248→\tfor {\n   249→\t\tselect {\n   250→\t\tcase tick := <-t.C:\n   251→\t\t\t// We use Round(0) on the start time to remove the monotonic clock.\n   252→\t\t\t// This is required as ticks from the ticker and time.Now() can have\n   253→\t\t\t// a monotonic clock that when subtracted do not represent the delta\n   254→\t\t\t// in wall clock time.\n   255→\t\t\tstart := time.Now().Round(0)\n   256→\t\t\tsch.metrics.BehindSeconds.Set(start.Sub(tick).Seconds())\n   257→\n   258→\t\t\tsch.processTick(ctx, dispatcherGroup, tick)\n   259→\n   260→\t\t\tsch.metrics.SchedulePeriodicDuration.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n   261→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   262→\t\t\t// waiting for all rule evaluation routines to stop\n   263→\t\t\twaitErr := dispatcherGroup.Wait()\n   264→\t\t\treturn waitErr\n   265→\t\t}\n   266→\t}\n   267→}\n   268→\n   269→type readyToRunItem struct {\n   270→\truleRoutine Rule\n   271→\tEvaluation\n   272→}\n   273→\n   274→// TODO refactor to accept a callback for tests that will be called with things that are returned currently, and return nothing.\n   275→// Returns a slice of rules that were scheduled for evaluation, map of stopped rules, and a slice of updated rules\n   276→func (sch *schedule) processTick(ctx On each tick, processTick() fetches alert rules from storage, determines which rules should evaluate based on their intervals, and dispatches evaluation jobs.\\n\\n**Rule Evaluation**: Each alert rule is represented by the alertRule struct in schedule/alert_rule.go. The Run() method creates an evaluation loop that listens for evaluation signals. When a rule needs evaluation, the evaluate() method is called, which:\\n  1. Creates an evaluator via evalFactory.Create() using the rule's condition\\n  2. Calls ruleEval.Evaluate() from eval/eval.go to execute the query/expression pipeline\\n  3. Passes results to stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()\\n\\n**State Transition**: The state/manager.go file implements Manager which handles alert state transitions through ProcessEvalResults(). This method:\\n  1. Calls setNextStateForRule() to determine new states based on evaluation results\\n  2. Uses State.transition() from state/state.go to perform state transitions (e.g., Normal→Alerting→Resolved)\\n  3. Updates LastSentAt timestamps for states that need sending\\n  4. Persists state changes to the database\\n  5. Invokes a callback to send state transitions\\n\\n**Notification Dispatch**: The send() method in alert_rule.go converts state transitions to PostableAlerts and calls alertsSender.Send(). This is implemented by AlertsRouter in sender/router.go, which:\\n  1. Routes alerts to the internal AlertManager via MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor(orgID)\\n  2. Calls alertmanager.PutAlerts() from notifier/alertmanager.go to inject alerts into the alertmanager\\n  3. Also routes alerts to external Alertmanagers if configured\\n\\n**Alert Manager**: The notifier/alertmanager.go and notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go files implement the Alertmanager interface. The PutAlerts() method converts alerts to the alerting/notify format and calls the underlying GrafanaAlertmanager.PutAlerts() to deliver alerts to configured receivers.\\n\\nThis chain ensures alert rules are periodically evaluated, state transitions are tracked, and notifications are dispatched through both internal and external alerting systems based on the organization's configuration.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":378,"cache_read_input_tokens":71617,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":378},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f47642a5-6b2f-4718-aa03-4fd3311db69e","uuid":"0aa92273-c17c-4457-8c8c-0fa81dfabf52"}
